  $(document).ready(function(){


 
/**************************************/
/***  Get specific list based on URL **/

//Get url entered
var url_data = window.location.href;

// check if specific list in url
if (url_data.indexOf("?list") > -1){

    // break url to get list name
    urlBreak = url_data.split("=");
    list = urlBreak[1];
    
   //Get list
   javascript:updateList(list);
}

         <div id="infoBox" style="padding: 10px; text-align: center;"> 

            <!-- Content that gets changed per selection -->
               <div id="info">
<img src="/media/contentassets/images/philanthropy/Copy of Philanthropy Report Scrolling Images (10)-1.png">
<p style="text-align:left;"> What an amazing year it has been at Muhlenberg. With new approaches in engagement thanks to a College-wide strategic plan, we broadened our scope and reach to all of you through enhanced programming. </p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> The impressive <a href="https://www.muhlenbergconnect.com/s/1570/index.aspx?sid=1570&gid=2&pgid=441">accomplishments of our alumni </a>this past year made us proud. From groundbreaking pediatricians to WWII historians, Muhlenberg graduates span the globe and the spectrum of contributions to the human condition. And proudly, our student/faculty collaborations resulted in <a href="https://www.muhlenbergconnect.com/s/1570/index.aspx?sid=1570&gid=2&sitebuilder=1&pgid=2794">undergraduate research </a>that rivals many of the nationâs top graduate programs in both the arts and sciences. </p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> Because of you, we raised over $2M for <a href="https://www.muhlenbergconnect.com/s/1570/index.aspx?sid=1570&gid=2&pgid=2802&sitebuilder=1&contentbuilder=1">The Muhlenberg Fund, </a>with alumni participation increasing every year - a strong sign of confidence and commitment. The Henry Melchior Muhlenberg Society grew to over 700 members, and the Parents Council contributed more than $167,000. Gifts to this fund are unrestricted, allowing the College to determine how best to support most programs on campus. For our students and faculty, this means that everything from financial aid to internships to research have a healthy reserve.</p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> Because of you, we saw a record turnout for <strong><em>#MULEMENTUM</em></strong>, our fifth annual day of giving in November 2017, <a href="https://www.muhlenbergconnect.com/s/1570/index.aspx?sid=1570&gid=2&sitebuilder=1&pgid=2775">for Alumni Reunion Weekend </a>in September 2017, and again for THAW in January 2018.</p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> Because of you, 87 percent of our students attend the College thanks to financial aid, which means we are recruiting the best and the brightest regardless of their ability to pay. Because of you, 86 percent of our students have a four-year graduation rate, which exceeds national retention by 25 percent. And because of you, more than 60 percent of our students learn from the world campus on a study abroad program, carrying the Muhlenberg tradition of excellence into communities far and near. </p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> On behalf of all Muhlenberg students, faculty and staff, I thank you for this banner year.</p>

<p style="text-align:left;"> Rebekkah L. Brown '99<br/>
Vice President, Advancement</p>

</div>

</div>

//check for ie
function isIE() {
    var ua = window.navigator.userAgent; //Check the userAgent property of the window.navigator object
    var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE '); // IE 10 or older
    var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/'); //IE 11

    return (msie > 0 || trident > 0);
}

//update to fix ie issue
function donorList(group) {
    if (isIE()) {
          url = "/impact/2018/?list=" + group;
          location.href = url;
       }
    else {
          updateList (group);
     }
}

function updateList(group){

//Close menu after selection
$('.sub_nav button').removeClass('fs-swap-active');
$('.sub_nav ul').removeClass('fs-swap-active');

//Update dropdown
var label = document.getElementsByClassName("sub_nav_handle_label");
var text;
if (group === "year"){
    text = "Alumni";
}   
else if (group === "parent"){
   text = "Parents";
}
else if (group === "friend"){
    text = "Friends";
}
else if (group === "facultyStaff"){
   text = "Faculty and Staff";
}
else if (group === "lifetime"){
  text = "Lifetime Giving Society";
}
else if (group === "henry"){
  text = "Henry Melchior Muhlenberg Society";
}
else if (group === "circle"){
   text = "Circle of 1848";
}
else if (group === "corporate"){
   text = "Corporate, Foundation and Government";
}
else if (group === "religious"){
   text = "Religious Organizations";
}
else if (group === "honor"){
   text = "In Honor and In Memory";
}
else if (group === "endowed"){
  text = "Endowed Funds";
}
else if (group === "volunteers"){
  text = "Muhlenberg Volunteers";
}
else {
 text = "Philanthropy Report";
}
label[0].innerHTML = text;

$('.sub_nav button').trigger('click');

//Jump to list on click

// Function to get year selected from dropdown 
function date(year){

//resize window
setTimeout(function(){
          $(window).resize();
      }, 500);


//must have a messages.php file to get year and pass back for ajax
$.ajax({
    url: "messages.php", 
    method: "post", 
    data: { "year":year},
    success: function(data){
    $('#body').html(data);
    
    },
     error: function() {
    alert('Not OKay');
    } 
   });

document.getElementById("yearList").innerHTML = "<br/><hr><h3 >Class of " + year + "</h3><br/><div id='body'></div>";

}
    
 </script>
